## PURPOSE

This exhibit catalogues documented incidents of parenting time interference,
denial, obstruction, and related conduct by the Defendant that has impacted
the Plaintiff's constitutionally protected parental relationship with the
minor child, L.D.W. Each incident is sourced from database records compiled
from court filings, transcripts, and documented communications.
